  142. # [00:29] <jez> - Note that (at least for now), multiplying string length by 2 results in the correct "byte length" for the string, because a UTF-32 character will actually be reported by .length as 2, rather than 1; 'xyz'.length basically gives the number of bytes used to hold the string divided by 2.
